## Summary

- Source candidates: 558 files (33462934 bytes) under `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root`.

- HSD model archives: 102; MDT message files: 6; raw BIN/PZZ layout or archive files: 9.
- Matching converted UI/menu outputs: 542. Public runtime currently has 2507 DAE and 3882 PNG files, but they are stage/borg exports, not these original UI groups.
- Current browser UI evidence: `apps/game/src/main.ts`, `apps/game/src/main.ts`, `apps/game/src/main.ts`, `apps/game/src/main.ts`, `apps/game/src/main.ts`.

## Blockers

- TPL textures: Standard TPL headers parse, but @gf/formats still has no decoder to emit PNG/KTX2 for titles, banners, portraits, thumbnails, or fonts. Refs: `packages/formats/src/tpl.ts:4`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/titles.tpl`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/bn0000.tpl`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/face0001.tpl`.
- UI/select/briefing model archives: HSD export pipeline exists for other assets, but vsel00/vsel01/brif00/entry00/face archives are not exported into browser public assets. Refs: `research/format-specs/arc-hsd-format.md:103`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/vsel00_mdl.arc`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/brif00_mdl.arc`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/entry00_mdl.arc`.
- Mission/menu text: msg*.mdt files are present, but the repo still needs an MDT text decoder/NeoGF mdttool integration before original copy can drive UI. Refs: `packages/formats/src/mdt.ts:3`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/msg00.mdt`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/sh_msg.mdt`.
- UI layout/control data: icon.bin, allbox.bin, trialbox.bin, plcmndata.bin, and comhit*.bin are raw-only until their schemas are mapped. Refs: `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/icon.bin`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/allbox.bin`, `user-data/GG4E/afs_data/root/comhit.bin`.
- Browser runtime UI: apps/game/src/main.ts contains hand-written DOM/CSS menu/HUD placeholders; those should not be extended as Adventure UI/HUD replacements. Refs: `apps/game/src/main.ts`, `apps/game/src/main.ts`, `apps/game/src/main.ts`.

## Preparation Path

- 1. Texture manifest: Decode the parsed TPL families to browser PNG/KTX2 and preserve source dimensions/formats in a UI texture manifest.
- 2. Model archive export: Batch-export vsel00/vsel01/brif00/entry00/face archives with the HSDRaw path used for stages/borgs, staged outside runtime source first.
- 3. Text extraction: Port or invoke NeoGF mdttool for msg*.mdt to produce message JSON before binding menus or briefings.
- 4. Layout/schema pass: Map icon.bin/allbox/trialbox/plcmndata/comhit schemas enough to place original sprites and HUD elements accurately.
- 5. Runtime replacement gate: Only replace the current fake DOM menu/HUD after the source assets above have converted outputs and verified screen-state mapping.

## Verification

- Re-run scanner: `rtk node scripts/inventory-ui-hud-assets.mjs`.
- JSON parse check: `rtk node -e "JSON.parse(require('fs').readFileSync('research/asset-inventory/ui-hud-assets.json','utf8')); console.log('json ok')"`.
- No browser source edit is performed by this inventory.
